146 * Please follow the instructions to add a new transaction field for this object Since we removed 
147 * the jGrinder and Transactional BO extension for this class. 
148 * 
149 * Step 1: add the ENUM in OrderTXFieldEnum class for the newly added field.
150 * Step 2: Modify the class OrderImplTXChangeLog to add the new field as a class variable and it's 
151 *         respective getter and setter for example:
152 *         
153 *    public double getTotalPrice()
154 *    {
155 *       return totalPrice;
156 *    }
157 *   
158 *    public void setTotalPrice(double p_totalPrice)
159 *    {
160 *       if(!TOTALPRICE.isBitSet(changeFieldBitMask))
161 *       {
162 *           changeFieldBitMask = TOTALPRICE.setBit(changeFieldBitMask);
163 *           totalPrice = p_totalPrice;
164 *       }
165 *    }
166 *    
167 *    Finally modifyt the rollbackChangesToParentTXLog method in OrderTXFieldEnum to add the check for this newly added field.
168 *
169 * For example Adding totalPrice as a Transaction field the setTotalPrice method will look like:
170 *     public void setTotalPrice(double newTotal) {
171 *       if (isBypassReflection())
172 *       {
173 *           totalPrice = newTotal;
174 *       }
175 *       else
176 *       {
177 *           getCurrentTXLog().setTotalPrice(this.totalPrice);
178 *           totalPrice = newTotal;
179 *       }
180 *     }
181 *
182 */
183 
184public class OrderImpl extends BaseDomainObjectImpl implements Order, OrderLocal

413    /**
414     * New constructor added for handling Light orders. 
415     * @author josephg
416     */
417        public OrderImpl (LightOrderEntry newOrder, SessionProfileUserStruct userStruct, TradingProduct product, String correspondent) throws DataValidationException,SystemException
418        {
419                 
420//                 initFromRequest(newOrder);
421                originalQuantity = newOrder.getQuantity();
422                userAssignedId = newOrder.getUserAssignedId();
423                cmtaExchange = newOrder.getCmtaExchange();
424        cmtaFirm = newOrder.getCmtaFirmNumber();
425        side = newOrder.getSide();
426        orderOriginType = (char) newOrder.getOriginCode();
427        userId = newOrder.getUserId();
428        userKey = findUserKey(newOrder.getUserId());
429        positionEffect = newOrder.getPositionEffect();
430        coverage = newOrder.getCoverage();
431        if (newOrder.isImmediateOrCancel())
432        {
433                contingency = ioc_contingency;
434        }
435        else
436        {
437                contingency = no_contingency;
438        }
439        price = newOrder.getPrice();
440        contingencyPrice = PriceFactory.create(PriceTypes.NO_PRICE, 0);        
441        boolean nbboProtected = newOrder.nbboProtectionOn();
442        if (nbboProtected)
443        {
444                orderNBBOProtectionType = OrderNBBOProtectionTypes.FULL;
445        }
446        else
447        {
448                orderNBBOProtectionType = OrderNBBOProtectionTypes.NONE;
449        }                
450        setHadNBBOProtection(nbboProtected); //TODO ???
451        setTransactionSequenceNumber(0);
452        String pdpm = newOrder.getPdpm();
453        if (pdpm != null && pdpm.length() > 0)
454        {
455                setExtensions(PDPMExtensionsCompatibleHelper.TIERED_PDPM_KEY + pdpm);
456        }
457        else
458        {
459                setExtensions("");
460        }
461        setLastBookedPrice(price);
462 
463        
464//                 initFromProfile (userStruct);
465                SessionProfileStruct lightOrderProfile = 
466                        UserProfileHelper.getUserProfileForClass(userStruct, product.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey(), product.getTradingClass().getSessionName());
467                
468        optionalData = "";
469        account = lightOrderProfile.account;
470        subaccount = lightOrderProfile.subAccount;
471        userAcronym = userStruct.userAcronym;
472        originator = userStruct.userAcronym;
473 
474                
475//                 initFromProduct (product);
476        activeSession = product.getTradingClass().getSessionName();
477                // create orderId by contacting ID service
478                orderKey = LightOrderUtils.generateOrderId();
479        UuidHolder uuid = new UuidHolder(orderKey);
480        sourceReceivedTime = System.currentTimeMillis(); //TODO or nano? also do we need this set?
481        
482        
483                orderId = new OrderIdStruct(lightOrderProfile.executingGiveupFirm, newOrder.getBranch(), 
484                                        newOrder.getBranchSequence(), correspondent, LightOrderUtils.getDate(sourceReceivedTime), uuid.getPrimaryBytes(),uuid.getSecondaryBytes());
485                classKey = product.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey();
486        productKey = product.getProductKey();
487 
488        productType = product.getTradingClass().getProductType();
489        sessionNames = new String[1];
490        sessionNames[0] = activeSession;
491                 
492//                 initCommonFields();
493                timeInForce = TimesInForce.DAY;
494                bookedQuantity = 0;
495        cancelledQuantity = 0;
496        tradedQuantity = 0;
497        bustedQuantity = 0;
498        source = Sources.LIGHT; 
499                
500        ohsReceivedTime = 0;
501        addedQuantity = 0;
502        orsId = "";
503        setBookedTime(0L);
504        setBookedStatus(0);
505        setWidenPrice(null); // this is initialized in OrderHomeImpl.setTransientValues to noPrice first
506        setShipQuantityWithoutPublishing(0);
507        setMarketAlertPublished(false);
508        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
509        setPendingTradePrice(null);
510        setPendingTradeId(0);
511        setInvolvedInQuoteTrigger(false);
512        setCancelRequestPending(false);
513        setPendingCancelRequestUserAssignedId(null);
514        setPendingCancelQuantity(0);
515        setCancelReplaceNewOrder(null);
516        markForDropCopy(false);
517        setBookedByAuction(false);
518        setInitialTradePrice(null);
519        setOddLotFlashedQuantity(0);
520 
521        setFillType(SubActivityType.DEFAULT);
522        markAuctionStarted(false);
523        setMarkedCancelReason((short)0);
524        setState(OrderStates.ACTIVE); //TODO what state to start with?
525        legOrderDetails = emptyLegDetails;
526        
527        }

529    /**
530     * This method populates the Order attributes that make an Order unique. Attributes that are part of the Order ID
531     * author Silvia Torres
532     */
533    private void setNonUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)
534            throws DataValidationException,SystemException
535    {
536        activeSession = newValues.activeSession;
537        timeInForce = newValues.timeInForce;
538        orderId = newValues.orderId;
539        classKey = newValues.classKey;
540        originalQuantity = newValues.originalQuantity;
541        userAssignedId = newValues.userAssignedId;
542        ohsReceivedTime = newValues.ohsReceivedTime;
543        sourceReceivedTime = newValues.sourceReceivedTime;
544        side = newValues.side;
545        setOrderSide(newValues.side);
546        source = newValues.source;
547        orderOriginType = newValues.orderOriginType;
548        addedQuantity = newValues.addedQuantity;
549        coverage = newValues.coverage;
550        originator = newValues.originator;
551        orsId = newValues.orsId;
552        positionEffect = newValues.positionEffect;
553        productKey = newValues.productKey;
554        productType = newValues.productType;
555        subaccount = newValues.subaccount;
556        userId = newValues.userId;
557        sessionNames = newValues.sessionNames;
558        contingency = newValues.contingency;
559        orderNBBOProtectionType = newValues.orderNBBOProtectionType;
560        userKey = findUserKey(newValues.userId);
561        contingencyPrice = PriceFactory.create(newValues.contingency.price);
562        orderKey = CboeId.longValue(new CboeIdStruct(newValues.orderId.highCboeId, newValues.orderId.lowCboeId));
563        userAcronym = findUser(newValues.userId).userAcronym;
564    }
565 
566   protected SessionProfileUserStruct findUser(String userId) throws SystemException, DataValidationException
567    {
568        try
569        {
570            return BusinessServicesHelper.getUserService().getSessionProfileUserInformation(userId);
571        }
572        catch (AuthorizationException ex)
573        {
574            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Authorization exception finding user by id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
575        }
576        catch (NotFoundException ex)
577        {
578            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid user id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
579        }
580        catch (CommunicationException ex)
581        {
582            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Communication exception finding user by id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
583        }
584    }
585 
586    /**
587     * The update Order process must be consistent with TPF. So, the only fields that need
588     * to be updated and checked are Optional data, Account and cmta.
589     * author Silvia Torres
590     */
591    private void setUserUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)
592    {
593        setOptionalData( newValues.optionalData );
594        setAccount( newValues.account );
595        setSubAccount(newValues.subaccount);
596        setCmtaExchange( newValues.cmta.exchange );
597        setCmta( newValues.cmta.firmNumber );
598    }
599 
600    private void setSystemUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct order)
601    {
602        // persisted field
603        setCancelledQuantity(order.cancelledQuantity);
604        setTradedQuantity(order.tradedQuantity);
605        setHadNBBOProtection(order.hadNBBOProtection);
606        setState(order.state);
607        setPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.price));
608        setLastBookedPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.effectivePrice));
609        setTransactionSequenceNumber(order.transactionSequenceNumber);
610        setExtensions(order.extensions);
611        setBustedQuantity(order.bustedQuantity);
612 
613        setBookedTime(0L);
614        setBookedStatus(0);
615        setWidenPrice(null); // this is initialized in OrderHomeImpl.setTransientValues to noPrice first
616        setShipQuantityWithoutPublishing(0);
617        setMarketAlertPublished(false);
618        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
619        setPendingTradePrice(null);
620        setPendingTradeId(0);
621        setInvolvedInQuoteTrigger(false);
622        setCancelRequestPending(false);
623        setPendingCancelRequestUserAssignedId(null);
624        setPendingCancelQuantity(0);
625        setCancelReplaceNewOrder(null);
626        markForDropCopy(false);
627        setBookedByAuction(false);
628        setInitialTradePrice(null);
629        setBookedQuantity(0);
630        setOddLotFlashedQuantity(0);
631 
632        setFillType(SubActivityType.DEFAULT);
633        markAuctionStarted(false);
634        setMarkedCancelReason((short)0);
635 
636        if(!order.handlingInstruction.equals(""))
637        {
638            HandlingInstruction handlingInstructionImpl = new OrderHandlingInstructionNoReflectionImpl();
639            handlingInstructionImpl.updateFrom(order.handlingInstruction, getQuantity());
640            setHandlingInstruction(handlingInstructionImpl);
641            expressOrder = handlingInstructionImpl.isExpressOrder();
642            this.inboundISOEnabled = handlingInstructionImpl.isInboundISOEnabled();
643            setBookableOrderMarketLimit(handlingInstructionImpl.getBookableOrderMarketLimit());
644        }
645    }

647    public void acceptOrderUpdateFromSync(OrderHandlingStruct order) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
648    {
649        // persisted field
650        setCancelledQuantity(order.cancelledQuantity);
651        setTradedQuantity(order.tradedQuantity);
652        setHadNBBOProtection(order.hadNBBOProtection);
653        setState(order.state);
654        setPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.price));
655        setLastBookedPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.effectivePrice));
656        setTransactionSequenceNumber(order.transactionSequenceNumber);
657        setExtensions(order.extensions);
658        setBustedQuantity(order.bustedQuantity);
659 
660        if(!order.handlingInstruction.equals(""))
661        {
662            HandlingInstruction handlingInstructionImpl = new OrderHandlingInstructionNoReflectionImpl();
663            handlingInstructionImpl.updateFrom(order.handlingInstruction, getQuantity());
664            setHandlingInstruction(handlingInstructionImpl);
665            expressOrder = handlingInstructionImpl.isExpressOrder();
666            this.inboundISOEnabled = handlingInstructionImpl.isInboundISOEnabled();
667            setBookableOrderMarketLimit(handlingInstructionImpl.getBookableOrderMarketLimit());
668        }     
669        setOptionalData( order.optionalData );
670        setAccount( order.account );
671        setSubAccount(order.subaccount);
672        setCmtaExchange( order.cmta.exchange );
673        setCmta( order.cmta.firmNumber );
674    }
675    
676    /**
677     * Set all fields of the persistent OrderImpl from a given OrderStruct.
678     * <p/>
679     * author Steven Sinclair
680     *
681     * @param order com.cboe.businessServices.interfaces.orderHandlingService.OrderStruct
682     */
683    public void setOrder(OrderHandlingStruct order) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
684    {
685        setNonUpdateableValues(order);
686        setSystemUpdateableValues(order);
687        setUserUpdateableValues(order);
688    }

727    public String getExecutingBroker()
728    {

733            {
734                Log.debug(this, "getExecutingBroker for I-Order: " + toString() + " use originator: " + getOriginatorAcronym().acronym);
735            }

744    private int getOriginalQuantity(boolean noCalculation)
745    {
746        if(noCalculation) return originalQuantity;
747

751        }

753    }

760    /**
761     * if the quanity is defined in the extensions field use it.
762     * @return
763     */
764    private int getCrossProductLegOrderQuantity()
765    {
766        try
767        {
768            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(getExtensions());
769            String strQuantityToTrade = extensionsHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_QUANTITY);
770            if(strQuantityToTrade != null)
771            {    
772                return Integer.parseInt(extensionsHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_QUANTITY));
773            }
774        }
775        catch(Exception e)
776        {
777            // no need to worry about this since it might not be set.
778        }
779        return originalQuantity;
780    }
781    
782    public int getCrossProductRatioQuantity()
783    {
784        if (crossProductRatioQuantity != 0)
785        {
786            return crossProductRatioQuantity;
787        }
788        
789        if(isCrossProductLegOrder())
790        {
791            try
792            {
793                ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(getExtensions());
794                String strQuantityToTrade = extensionsHelper.getValue(InternalExtensionFields.EQUITY_LEG_RATIO_QTY);
795                if(strQuantityToTrade != null)
796                {    
797                    crossProductRatioQuantity = Integer.parseInt(extensionsHelper.getValue(InternalExtensionFields.EQUITY_LEG_RATIO_QTY));
798                    return crossProductRatioQuantity;
799                }
800            }
801            catch(Exception e)
802            {   
803                //no need to worry about this since it might not be set.
804                if(Log.isDebugOn())
805                {
806                    Log.debug("OrderImpl.getCrossProductRatioQuantity> Ratio not already set.");
807                }
808            }
809        }
810        return 0;  
811    }

950    public void setState(short aValue) 
951    {
952        short oldState = getState();
953        if (isBypassReflection())
954        {
955            state = aValue;
956        }
957        else
958        {
959            getCurrentTXLog().setState(this.state);
960            state = aValue;
961        }
962 
963        if (oldState != 0) // Since if it setting the state at creation of OrderImpl object we do
964            // not
965            // want to call this mthod.
966            publishInternalStateChange(oldState, aValue);
967        //If the remaining quantity is less than or equal to zero add it to a list to be removed later
968        //this will take care of deleting ONLY cancelled orders
969        if (getRemainingQuantity() <= 0 && getTradedQuantity() <=0) {
970                        try {
971                                getTradingClass(getClassKey()).addToToBeRemovedOrders(this);
972                        } catch (DataValidationException e) {
973                                Log.alarm("Unable to get TradingClass" + e);
974                        }
975        }
976    }

1563/**
1564 * Gets time contingency status.  Only currently supported time continengencies
1565 * (for orders traded in SBT) are IOC, FOK.  If boolean to ignore handling instruction, the
1566 * real contingency type will be returned, otherwise will return it based on the handing instruction.
1567 * 
1568 */
1569public boolean hasTimeContingency(boolean ifConsiderHandlingInstruction) {
1570    if (ifConsiderHandlingInstruction && getHandlingInstruction() != null && getHandlingInstruction().ignoreContingency()) {
1571        return false;
1572    }
1573    return getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.IOC || getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.FOK;
1574}
1575/**
1576 * Gets volume contingency status.  Only currently supported volume continengencies
1577 * (for orders traded in SBT) are AON and FOK.  If boolean to ignore handling instruction, the
1578 * real contingency type will be returned, otherwise will return it based on the handing instruction.
1579 * 
1580 */
1581public boolean hasVolumeContingency(boolean ifConsiderHandlingInstruction) {
1582    if (ifConsiderHandlingInstruction && getHandlingInstruction() != null && getHandlingInstruction().ignoreContingency()) {
1583        return false;
1584    }
1585    return getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.AON || getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.FOK;
1586}

1630public void acceptedByBook(long aBookedTime, Price bookedPrice, boolean silent)
1631{
1632    acceptedByBook(aBookedTime, bookedPrice, false, silent);
1633}
1634 
1635public void acceptedByBook(long aBookedTime, Price bookedPrice, boolean isExternalUpdate, boolean silent)
1636{
1637        Price initialValue = getLastBookedPrice();
1638        Price finalValue = bookedPrice;
1639        setLastBookedPrice(bookedPrice);
1640     
1641        if(!silent)
1642        {
1643            setHandlingInstruction(null); //after booked, original handling instruction should not used
1644        }
1645        
1646    // will be accepted by book each time recovery is done, only need to
1647    // create booked history and publish if quantity is changing
1648 
1649        // only update the state if is booked at CBOEDirect.  Do not update state for external book since we did not book it here
1650            if (!isExternalUpdate)
1651        {
1652            setState(OrderStates.BOOKED);
1653        }
1654 
1655        // Check the flag to see if order needs to publish book event and store history
1656                      
1657        boolean isStopOrder = getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP
1658            || getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP_LIMIT
1659        || getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP_LOSS;
1660        
1661        boolean isToPublishToExternal = (!silent) && (needPublishBookedEvent() || isStopOrder || (!finalValue.equals(initialValue)));
1662           
1663        if ( isToPublishToExternal) 
1664        {
1665                incrementSequenceNumber();
1666                OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs = buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();
1667                getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptedByOrderBook.getEventType()).acceptedByOrderBook(
1668                                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1669                                getOrderId(), OrderStates.BOOKED,
1670                                getOrderBookUpdateStruct(), 
1671                                isToPublishToExternal, getPrimitiveProductKey(), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1672                                ordHistoryStructs);
1673                setNeedPublishBookedEvent(false);
1674        }
1675 
1676        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1677        {
1678            Log.debug(this, "OrderAcceptedByBook, UserId: " + getUserId() + "  Order Id: " + orderIdToString(getOrderId()));
1679        }
1680        }
1681 
1682/**
1683     * This method publishes the intermediate Order states over the IOSC to OHS.
1684     * @param oldState
1685     * @param newState
1686     */
1687    private void publishInternalStateChange(short oldState, short newState)
1688    {
1689        /**
1690         * If the state is routed away then return
1691         */
1692        if(newState == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY) {
1693            return;
1694        }
1695        if( (oldState != newState) && (newState != OrderStates.BOOKED &&
1696                                       newState != OrderStates.ACTIVE &&
1697                                       newState != OrderStates.CANCEL &&
1698                                       newState != OrderStates.FILL))
1699        {
1700            com.cboe.idl.order.OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ordDetails = buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();
1701            getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptInternalStateUpdate.getEventType()).acceptInternalStateUpdate(
1702                    getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1703                    getOrderId(), newState, getPrimitiveProductKey(), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1704                    ordDetails);            
1705        }
1706    }

1718 
1719    /**
1720     * parTradeMMSideBust will come from the BustReportManager. This will tell the order if the bust if coming
1721     * from a par trade and is the market maker executing the bust.  For these trade busts we do not want to publish
1722     * the bust report to the CMI user, however we want to publish the bust report to OHS so that a notification
1723     * can be sent to the OMT through the ReportWorkflow
1724     */
1725    public void bust(BustReportStruct bustInfo, TradeReport tradeReport, boolean parTradeMMSideBust) throws DataValidationException
1726    {
1727        // add this order to the cache so when it is reinstated, it will look at the same copy or the orderimpl
1728        // otherwise the reinstate will look at the database copy.
1729//        addOrderToCache();        
1730        if (bustInfo.productKey == getPrimitiveProductKey())
1731        {
1732                doOrderBust(bustInfo);
1733                bustInfo.bustReportType = getReportType();
1734        }
1735        else
1736        {
1737                doLegBust(bustInfo);
1738                bustInfo.bustReportType = ReportTypes.STRATEGY_LEG_REPORT;
1739        }
1740        bustInfo.transactionSequenceNumber = incrementSequenceNumber();
1741        publishBustReport(bustInfo, tradeReport, parTradeMMSideBust);
1742    }
1743

1745     * This method will bust the specifed quantity.  This reduces traded quantity and increase busted quantity
1746     */
1747    public void bust(BustReportStruct bustInfo, TradeReport tradeReport) throws DataValidationException
1748    {
1749        bust(bustInfo, tradeReport, false); // false should always publish the bust report out from TE.
1750    }

1756 
1757    /**
1758    * do order bust
1759    */
1760    private void doOrderBust(BustReportStruct bustInfo) throws DataValidationException
1761    {
1762                int quantity = bustInfo.bustedQuantity;
1763        if (quantity > getTradedQuantity())
1764        {
1765            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot bust more than the traded quantity",
1766                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
1767        }
1768        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1769        {
1770            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] Execute a bust on order for quantity " + quantity);
1771            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] traded/bust/cancelled is currently " + getTradedQuantity() + "/" + getBustedQuantity() + "/" + getCancelledQuantity());
1772        }
1773        setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() - quantity);
1774        setBustedQuantity(getBustedQuantity() + quantity);
1775        setCancelledQuantity(getCancelledQuantity() + quantity); //Since busted is no longer used in calculating remains, the cancelled quantity is incremented to account for the change.
1776        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1777        {
1778            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] traded/bust/cancelled adjusted to " + getTradedQuantity() + "/" + getBustedQuantity() + "/" + getCancelledQuantity());
1779        }
1780        }
1781 
1782        /**
1783         * find the leg detail and ask it to finish the leg bust
1784         */
1785    private void doLegBust(BustReportStruct bustInfo) throws DataValidationException
1786    {
1787        try
1788        {
1789                        LegOrderDetailImpl legDetail = (LegOrderDetailImpl) findOrderDetailForLeg(bustInfo.productKey);
1790                        legDetail.bust(bustInfo);
1791                }
1792        catch (Exception e)
1793        {
1794            Log.exception("can not do leg bust (product key is " + bustInfo.productKey + ")", e);
1795                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Can not do leg bust for order " + getOrderIdString(), 0);
1796                }
1797        }
1798 
1799// CBOEdirect Stock System uses this to identify Order from ITS.
1800//10/21/02 Ravi Rade Added to check if order is a linkage order.
1801 
1802public boolean isLinkageOrder()
1803{
1804    boolean linkageOrder = false;
1805    final char originType = getOrderOriginType();
1806    final char theSource = getSource();    
1807    if (getActiveSession().equals(CBSX_SESSION))  {
1808        if ((getUserAssignedId() != null) &&
1809            getUserAssignedId().equals(Order.SYSTEM_LINK_ORDER_USER_ASSIGNED_ID))  {
1810            linkageOrder = true;
1811        }
1812        else if (((originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL) ||
1813                (originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT)) &&
1814                (theSource == Sources.ITS))  {
1815            linkageOrder = true;                   
1816        }
1817    }
1818    else {
1819        if (originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL ||
1820                originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT ||
1821                originType == OrderOrigins.SATISFACTION)  {
1822            linkageOrder = true;
1823        }
1824    }
1825    return linkageOrder;
1826}

1906    {

1919        /**
1920         * publish cancel reports
1921     * <p/>
1922         * Note: cancelRequestId is only used for order which had NBBO protection.
1923         *       for normal cancel, it should be set to 0
1924         * @param p_reportsUnconditionally 
1925         */
1926    public void publishCancelReports(CancelReportStruct[] reports, short cancelReason, long cancelRequestId, boolean p_reportsUnconditionally)
1927    {
1928        long activityTime = System.currentTimeMillis(); 
1929        for(CancelReportStruct report : reports)
1930        {
1931            adjustTotalSessionCancelledQuantity(report.cancelledQuantity);
1932        }
1933        if ( ( isLightOrder() && getMyHome().shouldPublishCxlReportForLightOrder(cancelReason) ) || 
1934                        ( !isLightOrder() && getOrderOriginType() != InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER && !isLinkedAwayOrder() && !isLegDerivedOrder() ) )
1935        {
1936            getMyHome().getExtOrderStatusPublisher().acceptCancelReport(this.getRoutingStruct().groups,  StatusUpdateReasons.NEW,
1937                    this.getOrderStruct(), reports, "");
1938        }
1939 
1940        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ohdStructs_emptyStruct = new OrderHistoryDetailStruct[0];
1941        
1942        
1943        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptCancelReport.getEventType()).acceptCancelReport(
1944                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1945                getOrderId(), OrderStates.CANCEL,
1946                orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1947                ohdStructs_emptyStruct, activityTime); 
1948        if (!isLightOrder() && (hadNBBOProtection() && cancelReason == ActivityReasons.USER) || needsDropCopyForLinkageOrders(reports[0].cancelReportType) || isMarkedForDropCopy())
1949        {
1950            getMyHome().publishIntermarketCancelReports(this, reports, cancelRequestId);
1951        }        
1952    }

1957        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptCancelReplaceReport.getEventType()).acceptCancelReplaceReport(
1958                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1959                getOrderId(), replacementOrder, OrderStates.CANCEL,
1960                orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1961                ohdStructs); 
1962        if ((hadNBBOProtection() && cancelReason == ActivityReasons.USER) || needsDropCopyForLinkageOrders(reports[0].cancelReportType) || isMarkedForDropCopy())

2029    final CancelReportStruct[] cancelLegs(CancelReportStruct spreadCxlRpt)
2030    throws DataValidationException
2031    {
2032            ProductStaticInfo spreadInfo = null;
2033            
2034            try
2035            {
2036                    spreadInfo = ((TradingProductImpl)getTradingProduct()).getProdInfo();
2037            }
2038            catch(Exception e)
2039            {
2040                    Log.exception("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this, e);
2041                       return new CancelReportStruct[] {spreadCxlRpt};
2042            }
2043                   CancelReportStruct[] reports = new CancelReportStruct[spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs.length+1];
2044                   reports[0] = spreadCxlRpt;
2045            try
2046               {                       
2047                       // in order to support buy/write, need to blindly get productKey from strategy impl...
2048                       for (int i = 0; i < reports.length-1; i++)
2049                       {
2050                               reports[i + 1] = cancelLeg(spreadCxlRpt.cancelReason,
2051                                               spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key,
2052                                               spreadCxlRpt.cancelledQuantity * spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legRatioQuantity,
2053                                               spreadCxlRpt.userAssignedCancelId);
2054                       }
2055                       return reports;
2056               }
2057               catch (Exception e)
2058               {
2059                       Log.exception("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this, e);
2060                       return reports;
2061                       //throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
2062               }
2063    }

2147    /**
2148     * This method is to reject a fill for OUTGOING Linkage Order.
2149     *
2150     * @param tradedQuantity
2151     * @param tradePrice
2152     * @param fillReportExtensions
2153     * @param rejectReason
2154     */
2155    public void rejectFill(int tradedQuantity, PriceStruct tradePrice, String fillReportExtensions, short rejectReason) throws DataValidationException
2156    {
2157        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2158        {
2159            Log.debug(this, "request to reject the fill for order:" + getOrderIdString());
2160        }
2161 
2162        try
2163        {
2164            ExtensionsHelper helper = new ExtensionsHelper(fillReportExtensions);
2165            String awayExchangeExecId = helper.getValue(ExtensionFields.AWAY_EXCHANGE_EXEC_ID);
2166            //if( awayExchangeExecId == null  || awayExchangeExecId.equals(EMPTY_STRING) || execTime == null || execTime.equals(EMPTY_STRING))
2167            if (awayExchangeExecId == null || awayExchangeExecId.equals(EMPTY_STRING))
2168            {
2169                Log.information("Invalid request to rejectFill for order id: " + getOrderIdString());
2170                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Reject fill must have away exchange exec id and execution receipt time", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TIME);
2171            }
2172 
2173            //iF rejection is because of stale execution then send the original order time also.
2174            if (rejectReason == ActivityReasons.STALE_EXECUTION)
2175            {
2176                DateWrapper date = new DateWrapper(getOHSReceivedTime());
2177                helper.setValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_ORDER_TIME, date.format(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME));
2178 
2179                fillReportExtensions = helper.toString();
2180            }
2181        }
2182        catch (java.text.ParseException e)
2183        {
2184            Log.exception(this, "Parse exception while parsing the reject fill for order " + getOrderIdString(), e);
2185        }
2186        catch (FormatNotFoundException e)
2187        {
2188            Log.exception(this, "Date Parse exception while parsing the reject fill for order " + getOrderIdString(), e);
2189        }
2190        FilledReportStruct fillReject = buildReportForRejectFill(tradedQuantity, tradePrice, fillReportExtensions, rejectReason);
2191        FilledReportStruct[] fillRejectStructs = new FilledReportStruct[1];
2192        fillRejectStructs[0] = fillReject;
2193        publishFilledReports(fillRejectStructs, false, true); // this is rejected by External
2194    }

2196    /**
2197     * This will build the filled report struct to reject the fill.
2198     *
2199     * @param tradedQuantity
2200     * @param tradePrice
2201     * @param fillReportExtensions
2202     * @param rejectReason
2203     */
2204private FilledReportStruct buildReportForRejectFill(int tradedQuantity, PriceStruct tradePrice, String fillReportExtensions, short rejectReason)
2205{

2207    report.account = getAccount();
2208    report.cmta = getCmtaFirm();
2209    report.contraParties = new ContraPartyStruct[0];
2210    report.executingBroker = getExecutingBroker();
2211    report.executingOrGiveUpFirm = getExecutingOrGiveUpFirmStruct();
2212    report.fillReportType = ReportTypes.FILL_REJECT;

2217    report.positionEffect = getPositionEffect();
2218

2299 
2300        /**
2301         * carry out the task to fill the order and return a filled report struct
2302         */
2303        private FilledReportStruct doOrderFill(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String executingBroker, char billingType)
2304            throws DataValidationException
2305    {
2306 
2307        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2308        {
2309            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] fill(quantity=" + totalQuantity + ", tradePrice=" + tradePrice.toDouble() + ", contraParties[" + (contraParties == null ? "null array" : "" + contraParties.length) + "])");
2310            }
2311            FilledReportStruct report = null;
2312            checkTradedQuantity(totalQuantity);
2313        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
2314        if (handlingInstruction != null)
2315        {
2316                int totalTraded = handlingInstruction.getTradedVolume() + totalQuantity;
2317                handlingInstruction.setTradedVolume(totalTraded);
2318                if ( ! handlingInstruction.isDefaultMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid()) {
2319                    handlingInstruction.setMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid(
2320                            handlingInstruction.getMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid() - totalQuantity);
2321                }
2322 
2323            }
2324            setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() + totalQuantity);
2325        if (getInitialTradePrice() == null)
2326        {
2327                setInitialTradePrice(tradePrice);
2328            }
2329        report = buildFilledReportStruct(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties, executingBroker, billingType);
2330        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2331        {
2332                Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got filled for " + totalQuantity + " contracts");
2333            }
2334        if (getRemainingQuantity() == 0)
2335        {
2336                setState(OrderStates.FILL);
2337            }
2338        
2339        // store filled report for cross product leg trading and spread to leg trade from STS
2340        try
2341        {
2342            if(isCrossProductLegOrder())
2343        {
2344            addFillReportToList(report);
2345 
2346            ExtensionsHelper helper = getExtensionsHelper(report.extensions, "for fill report");
2347            addValueToExtensionsHelper(helper, "" + FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.TAGNUMBER, FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.CBOE);
2348            report.extensions = helper.toString();
2349            }
2350            else if(isStrategy() && isRolledoutSpreadClass() && getTradingProduct().isProxy())
2351            {
2352                addFillReportToList(report);
2353            }
2354            
2355            
2356        }
2357        catch (NotFoundException e)
2358        {
2359            Log.alarm("TradingProduct is not found for product: " + this.productKey);
2360        }    
2361        
2362            return report;
2363        }

2365        /**
2366         * check the traded quantity
2367         */
2368        private void checkTradedQuantity(int tradeQuantity) throws DataValidationException
2369        {
2370            int remainingQForTrade = getRemainingQuantityForTrade();
2371        if (tradeQuantity > remainingQForTrade)
2372        {
2373                Log.alarm(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got a fill request for " + tradeQuantity + " contracts; it only has " + remainingQForTrade + " available.");
2374                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Traded quantity is greater than remaining quantity of the order", 0);
2375            }
2376        }

2396    /**
2397         * do a fill on one of the leg
2398         */
2399    private FilledReportStruct doLegFill(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String executingBroker, char billingType)
2400    {
2401        FilledReportStruct report = null;
2402        try
2403        {
2404                        LegOrderDetail legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(productKey);
2405            report = legDetail.fill(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties);
2406

2408            BillingStrategy.setBillingType(report, billingType);

2410            populateSpecialvalues(report, productKey);

2412            {
2413                addFillReportToList(report);
2414            }
2415                }
2416        catch (Exception e)
2417        {
2418                        Log.exception("not found the leg with product key = " + productKey + " of strategy " + getPrimitiveProductKey(), e);
2419                }
2420                return report;
2421        }

2462        private FilledReportStruct buildFilledReportStruct(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, short tradeContext, char billingType)
2463        {

2465        }

2467        /**
2468         * build the filled report struct based on the informtion supplied
2469         * to calculate leaves quantity, use the method getRemainingQuantityForFillReport
2470         * UD 03/07/04 ...
2471         */
2472    private FilledReportStruct buildFilledReportStruct(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String executingBroker, char billingType)
2473    {
2474            FilledReportStruct report = new FilledReportStruct();
2475            report.fillReportType = getReportType();
2476            report.tradeId = CboeId.toStruct(tradeId);
2477            report.productKey = productKey;
2478            report.tradedQuantity = totalQuantity;
2479            report.leavesQuantity = getRemainingQuantityForFillReport();
2480            report.price = adjustPriceForReport(tradePrice).toStruct();
2481            report.contraParties = contraParties;
2482            report.positionEffect = getPositionEffect();
2483            report.side = getSideValue();
2484            populateCommonValueForReport(report, executingBroker);
2485            BillingStrategy.setBillingType(report, billingType);
2486            return report;
2487        }
2488 
2489        /**
2490         * The trade price in the system will always be the price for the asDefinedSide
2491         * if the product is strategy. But when reporting the price to the user when order
2492         * gets filled, the sign of the price has to be adjusted according. That is:
2493         * if the side of the order is OppositeSide, then sign of the price reported to
2494         * user should be flipped
2495         */
2496    private Price adjustPriceForReport(Price tradePrice)
2497    {
2498        if (isOppositeSide() && tradePrice.isValuedPrice())
2499        {
2500                return PriceFactory.createValuedPrice (-1 * tradePrice.toDouble());
2501 
2502            }
2503            return tradePrice;
2504        }

2507         * determine the report type

2516                        }

2518        catch (Exception e)

2526        /**
2527         * Populate the fill report struct with some common value
2528         */
2529    private void populateCommonValueForReport(FilledReportStruct report, String executingBroker)
2530    {
2531        report.transactionSequenceNumber = incrementSequenceNumber();
2532        report.userId = getUserId();
2533        report.userAcronym = getUserAcronym();
2534        report.orsId = getOrsId();
2535        report.cmta = getCmtaFirm();
2536        report.account = getAccount();
2537        report.subaccount = getSubAccount();
2538        report.originator = getOriginatorAcronym(false);
2539        report.optionalData = getOptionalData();
2540        report.userAssignedId = getUserAssignedId();
2541        //report.extensions = getExtensions(); //-MW  probably, people desided just leave it empty 07/22/2002
2542        if (report.extensions == null)
2543        {
2544            report.extensions = "";
2545        }
2546        report.timeSent = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(new java.util.Date().getTime());
2547        report.executingOrGiveUpFirm = getClearingFirm();
2548        report.sessionName = getActiveSession();
2549        report.executingBroker = executingBroker;
2550        if (isICMOrder())
2551        {
2552            overrideFillReportWithProfile(report);
2553        }
2554        else if (clearsLikeQuote())
2555        {
2556                if ((getAccount() == null) || (getAccount().length() == 0))
2557                {
2558                    // just use the accout from profile then.
2559                    overrideFillReportWithProfile(report);
2560                }
2561        }
2562    }
2563 
2564        /**
2565         * return true if all legs' remaining quantity is zero. If this is a regular order, it
2566         * always return false(because there is no leg for regular order).
2567         */
2568    public boolean legsHaveRemainingQuantity()
2569    {
2570        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
2571        for (int i = 0; i < legs.length; i++)
2572        {
2573            if (legs[i].getLeavesQuantity() != 0)
2574            {
2575                return true;
2576            }
2577        }
2578        return false;
2579    }

2582     * Publish the FilledReports for internal fill by CBOE only
2583     */
2584    public void publishFilledReports(FilledReportStruct[] reports, String salePrefix)
2585    {
2586        // if the fills are for spread trade server enabled, spread leg trading, hold the fill publish
2587        // and let STS publish
2588        
2589        try
2590        {
2591            if (isStrategy() && isRolledoutSpreadClass() && getTradingProduct().isProxy())
2592                return;
2593        }
2594        catch (Exception e)
2595        {

2597            return;
2598        }

2600    }
2601 
2602    /**
2603     * Publish the FilledReports
2604     */
2605    public void publishFilledReports(FilledReportStruct[] reports, boolean internalFills, boolean publishReport)
2606    {
2607 
2608    // UD 10/08/04...
2609    // In QuoteTrigger condition, order's remaningQty doesn't match filled report
2610    // remaningQty on a parital fill, so need to calculate remaining qty of the order
2611    // as done for the filledOrderStruct.leavesQuantity ...
2612      
2613        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ohdStructs =  buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();  
2614        //OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ohdStructs =  buildOrderHistoryDetailStructsForFR();
2615        
2616        
2617    if(publishReport) {
2618        applyFillOnTheOrder(reports);
2619        if (!(getOrderOriginType() == InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER || isLinkedAwayOrder() || isLegDerivedOrder()))
2620        {
2621            getMyHome().getExtOrderStatusPublisher().acceptOrderFillReport(this.getRoutingStruct().groups,  StatusUpdateReasons.NEW, this.getOrderStruct(), reports, "");
2622        }
2623        
2624        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptFillReport.getEventType()).acceptFillReport(
2625                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
2626                getOrderId(), OrderStates.FILL,
2627                getFillsFromFillReports(reports), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
2628                ohdStructs);  
2629                
2630    }
2631        //The call to recordOrderExecution may or may not actually record the execution depending on the settings in the
2632        //OrderMarketMonitoringService configuration.
2633        try
2634        {
2635            if (needsDropCopyForLinkageOrders(reports[0].fillReportType) || isMarkedForDropCopy())
2636            {
2637                //An assumption is that every order that "hadNBBOProtection" will have had the execution recorded and therfore
2638                getMyHome().publishIntermarketFilledReports(this, reports);
2639            }
2640            else
2641            {
2642                getMyHome().getOrderMarketMonitoringService().recordOrderExecution(this, CboeId.longValue(reports[0].tradeId), reports);
2643            }
2644        }
2645        catch (Exception ex)
2646        {
2647            //Catching this exception here is a side effect of moving the recordOrderExecution to this method.
2648            //The publishIntermarketFilledReports has the same "catch-all" block so I had to keep the behavior
2649            //the same instead of propogating the exception.
2650            Log.alarm(this, "Cannot publish intermarket fill reports due to exception: " + ex);
2651        }
2652        // check if market alert needs to be published on the fill.  Only when it is filled for the first time at CBOEDirect we check.
2653        if (internalFills
2654                && getMyHome().shouldPublishMarketAlertOnOriginType(getOrderOriginType())
2655                && !hasMarketAlertPublishedBefore()
2656                && getRemainingQuantity() > 0)
2657        {
2658            marketAlertPublished = true;
2659            // comment cout since they are not sure what to do with this yet 4-23-04 Connie
2660            //getMyHome().getMarketAlertPublisher().acceptMarketAlert(getRoutingStruct(), getMarketAlertStruct(reports[0].timeSent));
2661        }
2662 
2663    }
2664 
2665    /**
2666     * Determine if this order needs drop copy.
2667     *
2668     * @param reportTypes
2669     */
2670    private boolean needsDropCopyForLinkageOrders(short reportTypes)
2671    {
2672        //Fill/cancel report for Incoming satisfaction order. 
2673        // || If away exchange rejects the fill sent by CBOE, for an incoming linkage order.
2674        return isIncomingLinkageOrder() &&
2675            (  getOrderOriginType() == OrderOrigins.SATISFACTION
2676               || reportTypes == ReportTypes.FILL_REJECT );
2677    }

2833    /**

3061 
3062    /**
3063     * Return the part of the total quantity which is allowed to trade.
3064     * <p/>
3065     * Note: getQuantity() should return the total available quantity of a tradable.
3066     *      but in a particular trade, we may only want to trade with a partial of
3067     *      the total available quantity, which is specified by the result of getQuantityAllowable()
3068     */
3069    public int getQuantityAllowed()
3070    {
3071        if(!calculateQuantityAllowed)
3072        {
3073            //If this flag is set to false we just want to return back with 0 so that it cannot take part in trading.
3074            return 0;
3075        }
3076        // Check if Max AutoEx Quantity should be used. If MaxQuantity is set to default means, we never
3077        // touched it so skip any further logic.
3078        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
3079        if (handlingInstruction != null &&
3080            ! handlingInstruction.isDefaultMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid() )
3081        {
3082            int maxRemainingQuantity = handlingInstruction.getMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid();
3083            if (maxRemainingQuantity < getRemainingQuantityForTrade() ) 
3084            {
3085                return maxRemainingQuantity;
3086            } 
3087        }
3088 
3089        return getRemainingQuantityForTrade();
3090    }

3099            setNeedPublishBookedEvent(true);
3100    }
3101 
3102    /**
3103     * This method calculates the order's remaining quantity for Fill Report.
3104     * 03/08/04...
3105     * author Uma Diddi
3106     *
3107     * @return int
3108     */
3109    public int getRemainingQuantityForFillReport()
3110    {
3111        return getOriginalQuantity(true) +
3112                getAddedQuantity() -
3113                getTradedQuantity() -
3114                getCancelledQuantity();
3115    }
3116 
3117    /**
3118     * This method calculates the orders remaining quantity allowed for trade.
3119     * The remaining quantity for trade may differ from the actual remaining quantity
3120     * but should be less than or equal to the actual remaining quantity
3121     */
3122    public int getRemainingQuantityForTrade()
3123    {
3124            int remainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
3125        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
3126        if (handlingInstruction == null)
3127        {
3128            return remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity() - getOddLotFlashedQuantity();
3129        }
3130 
3131        short tradingRestriction = handlingInstruction.getTradingRestriction();
3132        int allowedQ = 0;
3133        short handlingMode = handlingInstruction.getRemainderHandlingMode();
3134 
3135        // Because AIM is internalized order, maximumExecutionVolume is ignored; ship quantity is excluded for trade&ship
3136        if (handlingMode == RemainderHandlingModes.AUCTION_AND_RETURN_REMAINDER)
3137        {
3138            allowedQ = remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity();;
3139        }
3140        // for HAL order, maximumExecutionVolume is ignored; ship quantity is excluded for trade&ship
3141        else if (handlingMode == RemainderHandlingModes.HAL)
3142        {
3143            allowedQ = remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity();;
3144        }
3145        else if (tradingRestriction == TradingRestrictions.SWEEP_AND_RETURN)
3146        {
3147            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();;
3148        }
3149        else if (tradingRestriction == TradingRestrictions.FISH_AND_RETURN)
3150        {
3151            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();
3152        }
3153        else if (TradingRestrictions.NONE == tradingRestriction &&
3154                 handlingInstruction.getRemainderHandlingMode() == RemainderHandlingModes.RETURN_REMAINDER) {
3155            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();
3156        }
3157        else
3158        {
3159            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity();
3160        }
3161 
3162        if (allowedQ >= remainingQuantity)
3163        {
3164            return remainingQuantity;
3165        }
3166        return allowedQ;
3167    }

3357    LegOrderDetailStruct[] legDetailStructs = new LegOrderDetailStruct[strategyLegDetail.length];
3358        for (int i = 0; i < strategyLegDetail.length; i++)
3359    {
3360        legDetailStructs[i] = strategyLegDetail[i].toStruct();
3361    }
3362    order.legOrderDetails = legDetailStructs;
3363 
3364    return order;
3365}

3367/**
3368 * convert the internal state to external state
3369 */
3370    private short getExternalOrderState()
3371    {
3372    if (getState() == OrderStates.ACTIVE ||
3373        getState() == InternalOrderStates.ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT ||
3374        getState() == InternalOrderStates.IPP_EXPOSING ||
3375        getState() == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY ||
3376        getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_WAITING ||
3377        getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_EXPOSING)
3378    {
3379        return OrderStates.BOOKED;
3380    }
3381    else if(getState() == InternalOrderStates.INACTIVE_CANCEL_RE_REQUEST_PENDING)
3382    {
3383        return OrderStates.INACTIVE;
3384    }
3385 
3386    return getState();
3387}

3560public boolean isAuctionActive()
3561{
3562    boolean beingAuctioned = false;
3563    try
3564    {
3565        TradingProduct product = getTradingProduct();
3566        AuctionInternal auction  = product.getActiveAuction();
3567        if (auction != null)
3568        {
3569            AuctionBook auctionBook = auction.getAuctionBook();
3570            Order auctionedOrder = auctionBook.getAuctionedOrder();
3571            
3572            if (auctionedOrder == null)
3573            {
3574                return false;
3575            }
3576            long auctionedOrderId = auctionedOrder.getUniqueId();
3577            if (auctionedOrderId == this.getUniqueId())
3578            {
3579                beingAuctioned = true;
3580            }  
3581        }
3582    }
3583    catch (NotFoundException nfe)
3584    {
3585        beingAuctioned = false;
3586    }
3587    return beingAuctioned;
3588}

3590/**
3591 * Determins if this order can be reinstated after a bust
3592     *
3593 * @return boolean
3594 */
3595public boolean isReinstatable()
3596{
3597    if (isMinSizeGuaranteeOrder() || treatedLikeQuote() || isAuctionActive()) {
3598 
3599        return false;
3600    }
3601    short contingencyType = getContingencyType();
3602    if (contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.CLOSE ||
3603            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP ||
3604            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.OPG) {
3605        return true;
3606    }
3607    if (contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.NONE ||
3608            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.AON ||
3609            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.RESERVE ||
3610            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP_LOSS ||
3611            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP_LIMIT || 
3612            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP_BOOK)
3613        {
3614            if (!getPrice().isMarketPrice())
3615            {
3616            return true;
3617        }
3618    }
3619    return false;
3620}

3657    public static String orderIdToString(OrderIdStruct orderId)
3658{
3659    String result;
3660        if (orderId.highCboeId != 0)
3661        {
3662        result = orderId.highCboeId + ":" + orderId.lowCboeId;
3663    }
3664        else
3665        {
3666        String orderDate = "";
3667        try
3668        {
3669                orderDate = orderId.orderDate.equals("") ? (new DateWrapper()).format("OrderDate") : orderId.orderDate;
3670        }
3671            catch (com.cboe.util.FormatNotFoundException e)
3672        {
3673            Log.alarm("orderIdToString: No OrderDate available for order :" +
3674                orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange + ":" +
3675                orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber + ":" +
3676                orderId.branch + ":" +
3677                orderId.branchSequenceNumber + ":" +
3678                orderId.correspondentFirm
3679                );
3680        }
3681        result =  orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange + ":" +
3682            orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber + ":" +
3683            orderId.branch + ":" +
3684            orderId.branchSequenceNumber + ":" +
3685            orderId.correspondentFirm + ":" +
3686            orderDate;
3687    }
3688    return result;
3689}

3793    /**
3794    *  Will reinstate the quantity specified.  This has the net effect of increasing remaining quantity by the specified quantity.
3795     *
3796    *  @param quantity  The quantity to reinstate
3797     * @throws DataValidationException if quantity > bustedQuantity
3798    */
3799    public void reinstate(long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
3800    {
3801        if (quantity > getBustedQuantity())
3802        {
3803            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot reinstate more quantity than is busted",
3804                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
3805        }
3806        if (getState() == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY)
3807        {
3808            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot reinstate the order being at OMT/PAR/OHS.",
3809                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_ORDER_STATE);
3810        }
3811        if (!isActive())
3812        {
3813            setState(OrderStates.ACTIVE);
3814        }
3815        //Reduced busted quantity by the specified quantity, this will in effect raise remaining quantity.
3816        //setBustedQuantity(getBustedQuantity() - quantity);
3817        setCancelledQuantity(getCancelledQuantity() - quantity);
3818        if (propagateToOrderLegs())
3819        {
3820            reinstateLegs(quantity);
3821        }
3822 
3823                //Increase the sequence number before create history to avoid the duplicated order id in history
3824                incrementSequenceNumber();
3825        getMyHome().addOrderToCache(this);
3826        publishBustReinstateReport(tradeId, quantity);
3827    }
3828 
3829    /**
3830     * Updates the legs with the reinstated quantity.
3831     */
3832    private void reinstateLegs(int quantity) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
3833    {
3834            try
3835            {
3836                    ProductStaticInfo spreadInfo = ((TradingProductImpl)getTradingProduct()).getProdInfo();
3837                    for (int i = 0; i < spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs.length; ++i)
3838                    {
3839                            try
3840                            {
3841                                    // in order to support buy/write, need to blindly get productKey from strategy impl...
3842                                    LegOrderDetail legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key);
3843                                    legDetail.reinstate(quantity * spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legRatioQuantity);
3844                            }
3845                            catch (Exception e)
3846                            {
3847                                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Unable to reinstate on leg of prod["+spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key+"] for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
3848                            }
3849                    }
3850            }
3851            catch (NotFoundException e)
3852            {
3853                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Unable to reinstate for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
3854        }
3855    }
3856 
3857    /**
3858     *  This method will publish the reinstatement report to the event channel
3859     */
3860    public void publishBustReinstateReport(long tradeId, int quantity)
3861    {
3862 
3863        BustReinstateReportStruct report = new BustReinstateReportStruct();
3864 
3865        report.tradeId = CboeId.toStruct(tradeId);
3866        report.bustedQuantity = quantity;
3867        report.reinstatedQuantity = quantity;
3868        report.totalRemainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
3869        report.price = getPrice().toStruct();
3870        report.productKey = getPrimitiveProductKey();
3871        report.side = getSideValue();
3872        report.timeSent = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(new java.util.Date().getTime());
3873        report.transactionSequenceNumber = getTransactionSequenceNumber();
3874                report.sessionName = getActiveSession();
3875 
3876        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs =  buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();
3877        
3878        getMyHome().getOrderStatusPublisher().acceptOrderBustReinstateReport(
3879                        this.getRoutingStruct().groups, StatusUpdateReasons.NEW, this.getOrderStruct(), report, "");
3880        
3881        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptBustReinstateReport.getEventType()).acceptBustReinstateReport(
3882                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(), getOrderId(), StatusUpdateReasons.NEW,
3883                getBustReinstateFromBustReinstateReport(report), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
3884                ordHistoryStructs);
3885 
3886        if (Log.isDebugOn())
3887        {
3888            Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderId() + " got reinstate with " + quantity + " contracts");
3889        }
3890 
3891    }

3893    
3894    /**
3895     *  This method will publish the bust report to the event channel
3896     */
3897    private void publishBustReport(BustReportStruct bustInfo, TradeReport tradeReport, boolean parTradeMMSideBust)
3898    {
3899        BustReportStruct[] bustReports = new BustReportStruct[1];
3900        bustReports[0] = bustInfo;
3901        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ohdStructs =  buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();
3902        short statusChange = StatusUpdateReasons.NEW;
3903        
3904        // No longer needed as only MM side of PAR requires Bust Notification and which is taken care of in the BRM:bust

3958    /**

3965    {

3970                || isMarketOddLot() && treatedLikeQuote() || isPartOfCross())
3971        {
3972            return false;
3973        }
3974        else
3975        {
3976            return true;
3977        }
3978    }

3990    private int getIPPMinSize()
3991    {

3993        try
3994        {
3995            TradingClass tradingClass = getTradingProduct().getTradingClass();
3996            result = tradingClass.getTradingPropertyIPPMinSize();
3997        }
3998        catch (NotFoundException e)
3999        {
4000            Log.alarm("OrderImpl >>> Can not getIPPMinSize because trading product for " + getProductKey() + " is not found. Default: " + result);

4005    /**
4006    * Tells the tradable can now book itself if it OKs it
4007     * <p/>
4008    * author Connie Liang
4009    */
4010    public void handleBookProcessing(OrderBook book) throws DataValidationException
4011    {
4012            boolean booked = isBooked();
4013            if (booked)
4014            {
4015                    try
4016                    {
4017                       int qtyToUpdate = getQuantityAllowed()-getBookedQuantity();
4018                       if (qtyToUpdate!=0)
4019                            book.update(this, qtyToUpdate, true);
4020                    }
4021                    catch (Exception e)
4022                    {
4023                            Log.alarm("failed to find the booked order for update, just add it in: "+this);
4024                            resetBookedTime();
4025                            booked = false;
4026                    }
4027            }
4028            if (!booked && eligibleForBook()) {
4029            prevReservedQuantity=0;
4030            prevDisplayedQuantity = 0;
4031            prevRemainingQuantity=0;
4032            displayQuantity=0;
4033            book.acceptTradable(this);
4034        } else {
4035            postBookUpdateProcessing(this, null);
4036        }
4037    }
4038    /**
4039     *
4040     */
4041    public void postBookUpdateProcessing(OrderBook book)
4042        throws DataValidationException
4043    {
4044        postBookUpdateProcessing( this, book );
4045    }
4046 
4047    /**
4048    * Tells the tradable can now start to process its own logic
4049    * after the book is updated.
4050    *
4051    * @param Order is passed because there may be a DerivedOrder wrapping
4052    * this order in which case we need to unbook that one
4053    *
4054    * author Connie Liang
4055    */
4056    public void postBookUpdateProcessing(Order self, OrderBook book)
4057    throws DataValidationException
4058    {
4059        int myquantity = getQuantityAllowed();
4060 
4061        if( isMarketOddLot() && treatedLikeQuote() )
4062        {
4063            //When an order is Q-like, then we cancel when only an odd lot remains. 
4064                if (isBooked())
4065               unbookOrder(self, book, myquantity);
4066            cancel(ActivityReasons.INSUFFICIENT_QUANTITY);
4067        }
4068        else if( !eligibleForBook()   && myquantity != 0 && !isPartOfCross())
4069        {
4070 
4071            //Although when the order has been assigned to the NBBO Agent it is no longer
4072            //eligible for booking; however, in this case we won't want to cancel the order.
4073            
4074            String cancelStrategy = getBelowIPPMinSizeProcessingStrategy();
4075 
4076            if(cancelStrategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.CANCEL_ORDER_BELOW_IPP))
4077            {
4078                if(Log.isDebugOn())
4079                {
4080                    Log.debug(this, "Insufficient quantity. Need to cancel the order...");
4081                }
4082                if (isBooked())
4083                   unbookOrder(self, book, myquantity);
4084                cancel(ActivityReasons.INSUFFICIENT_QUANTITY);
4085            }
4086            else
4087            {
4088                // ??? Hmm, what about booking since the cancel strategy is not CANCEL_ORDER_BELOW_IPP
4089            }
4090        }
4091        else if( getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE && myquantity > 0 )
4092        {
4093            if( hasReserveQuantityDisplayed )
4094            {
4095                hasReserveQuantityDisplayed = false;
4096                // Keep the original state of the order before rebooking.
4097                short originalState = self.getState();
4098                
4099                // Rebook the order to make it lose priority.
4100            
4101                rebookOrder(self, book, myquantity );
4102                
4103                // The rebook is causing some orders to not be sent to autolink,
4104                // (when the displayQty was filled during the trade) 
4105                // To fix this, set the state of the order to the original state
4106                // before rebooking (IPP_EXPOSING), this way it will 
4107                // be sent to autolink.
4108                // (PITS 11751)
4109                if (self.isTradable(TradableTypes.NBBO_DERIVED_ORDER) &&
4110                    originalState == InternalOrderStates.IPP_EXPOSING)
4111                {
4112                    self.changeToState(originalState);
4113                }
4114            }
4115        }
4116        // if IOC I order then check below logic
4117        // check if the tradable is still either market against other side book,
4118        // or opposite auction price
4119        cancelIOCQuoteLikeOrder(self, true, book);
4120    }
4121 
4122    private boolean unbookOrder(Order self, OrderBook book, int cancelQuantity)
4123    {       
4124        if (cancelQuantity == 0)
4125                return false;
4126        
4127        //The book does not know about any odd lot portions for quote like orders
4128        if(book == null )
4129        {
4130            return false;
4131        }
4132 
4133        try
4134        {
4135            book.unbook(self, cancelQuantity, self.getSide(), self.getLastBookedPrice());
4136            return true;
4137        }
4138        catch(Exception e)
4139        {
4140            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when unbook the Order: " + e.toString());
4141            return false;
4142        }
4143    }
4144 
4145    /**
4146     * Rebook the order in the order book so that it loses priority
4147     */
4148    private void rebookOrder(Order self, OrderBook book, int quantity )
4149    {
4150        if(book == null)
4151        {
4152            return;
4153        }
4154 
4155        try
4156        {
4157                if (self.isBooked())
4158                {
4159               book.unbook(self, quantity, self.getSide(), self.getLastBookedPrice());
4160                }
4161        }
4162        catch(Exception e)
4163        {
4164            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when rebook::unbook the Order::"+self+" -- "+e.toString());
4165        }
4166        prevRemainingQuantity = 0;
4167        prevReservedQuantity = 0;
4168        prevDisplayedQuantity = 0;
4169        displayQuantity = 0;
4170 
4171        try
4172        {
4173            book.acceptTradable(self);
4174        }
4175        catch(Exception e)
4176        {
4177            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when rebook::rebook the Order::"+self+" -- "+e.toString());
4178        }
4179    }

4229    public void update(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)

4292    /**
4293     * Checks to see if the account need to be blanked.  For ALLSESSIONS profile,
4294     * we need to check if the xml configuration for the session is set.  Otherwise, use the
4295     * flag set in the profile for the user.
4296     *
4297     * @param profileStruct
4298     * @param currentAccount
4299     * @param userAcronym
4300     */
4301    private String checkBlankAccount(SessionProfileStruct profileStruct, String currentAccount, String userAcronym)
4302    {
4303        String account = currentAccount;
4304        boolean isAllSessions = SessionProfileHelper.isProfileForAllSessions(profileStruct);
4305        if (userAcronym.equalsIgnoreCase(currentAccount) && !isAllSessions && profileStruct.isAccountBlanked)
4306        {
4307            // we want to send blank account, when the flag is ON
4308            account = EMPTY_STRING;
4309            if (Log.isDebugOn())
4310            {
4311                Log.debug("Want to send blank account, when the profile flag is ON, for userAcronym: "
4312                                + userAcronym + " using profile:(" + profileStruct.sessionName + ":" + profileStruct.classKey + ":"
4313                                + profileStruct.account + ":" + profileStruct.subAccount + ":"
4314                                + profileStruct.executingGiveupFirm.exchange + "-" + profileStruct.executingGiveupFirm.firmNumber + ":"
4315                                + profileStruct.isAccountBlanked + ")");
4316            }
4317        }
4318        else if (isAllSessions && userAcronym.equalsIgnoreCase(currentAccount)
4319            && getMyHome().blankAccountIfSameAsAcr())
4320        {
4321            if (Log.isDebugOn())
4322            {
4323            Log.debug(this, "account is the same as the acronym.  Setting account to blank  " + account);
4324            }
4325            account = EMPTY_STRING;
4326        }
4327        return account;
4328    }

4330 /**

4345        }

4370            }
4371        }

4381    private void setBrokerAcronymForManulQuote(TradeReportEntry reportEntry) 
4382    {
4383        if (isManualQuote()) 
4384        {
4385            // get XXP from OrderHomeImpl
4386            String manualQuoteContraOrderBroker = getMyHome().getManualQuoteContraOrderBroker();
4387            ExchangeAcronymStruct manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym 
4388                = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(getUserAcronym().exchange, manualQuoteContraOrderBroker);
4389            
4390            // get XXH from OrderHomeImpl
4391            String anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker = getMyHome().getAnonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker(); 
4392            
4393            //set broker acronym to XXP for manual quote 
4394            //if the contra tradable is an order and its broker acronym is XXH 
4395            if (this.isBuySide() && (reportEntry.getSellOrderId() != 0) 
4396                    && (reportEntry.getSeller() != null) 
4397                    && (reportEntry.getSeller().acronym.equals(anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker)) )
4398                    reportEntry.setSeller(manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym);
4399            else if (this.isSellSide() && (reportEntry.getBuyOrderId() != 0) 
4400                    && (reportEntry.getBuyer() != null) 
4401                    && (reportEntry.getBuyer().acronym.equals(anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker)) )
4402                reportEntry.setBuyer(manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym);   
4403        }
4404    }

4410    {
4411        if (Log.isDebugOn())
4412        {

4414        }

4425            {

4427            }
4428        }

4475    {

4615        char sellSideIndicator = Sides.SELL;

4620            // such as leg of spread order and simple order. 
4621            sellSideIndicator = getSideValue();
4622        }
4623        reportEntry.setSellSideIndicator(sellSideIndicator);
4624    }
