4743 
4744    // NOTE For linkge phase II, this method must be re-visited.
4745    public FilledReportStruct linkageFill(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String reportExtensions) throws DataValidationException
4746    {
4747        FilledReportStruct report = null;
4748        int remainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
4749        String exchangeExecIdString = getExchangeExecIdString(reportExtensions);
4750        if (totalQuantity > remainingQuantity)
4751        {
4752            Log.alarm(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got a fill request for order=(" + getOrderIdString() +
4753                ") with exchange/execId=(" + exchangeExecIdString +
4754                totalQuantity + " contracts; it only has " + remainingQuantity + " available.");
4755            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Traded quantity in fill report exchange/execId=(" + exchangeExecIdString +
4756                ") is greater than remaining quantity of the order", 0);
4757        }
4758 
4759        //zero delta qty, no need to check book status
4760        setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() + totalQuantity);
4761        setShipQuantity(getShipQuantity() - totalQuantity);
4762 
4763        if (getInitialTradePrice() == null)
4764        {
4765            setInitialTradePrice(tradePrice);
4766        }
4767        
4768        char billingType = BillingStrategy.parseLinkageTradeBillingType(this);
4769        report = buildFilledReportStruct(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties, billingType);
4770        try
4771        {
4772            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(report.extensions == null ? "" : report.extensions);
4773            extensionsHelper.appendExtensions(reportExtensions);
4774            report.extensions = extensionsHelper.toString();
4775        }
4776        catch (ParseException e)
4777        {
4778            Log.exception(e);
4779        }
4780 
4781        //For rejecting the fill for an outgoing Satisfaction order we need to store exec id and reciept time
4782        //We are using UserAssignedId for that in order history.
4783        if (isLinkageOrder() && !isIncomingLinkageOrder() && getOrderOriginType() == OrderOrigins.SATISFACTION)
4784        {
4785            try
4786            {
4787                ExtensionsHelper helper = getExtensionsHelper(reportExtensions, "for report");
4788                DateWrapper date = DateWrapper.parse(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME, helper.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXECUTION_RECEIPT_TIME));
4789                DateWrapper expireTime = new DateWrapper(date.getTimeInMillis() + FILL_REJECT_TIME);
4790                addValueToExtensionsHelper(helper, ExtensionFields.EXPIRATION_TIME, expireTime.format(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME));
4791                report.extensions = helper.toString();
4792            }
4793            catch (Exception e)
4794            {
4795                Log.exception(this, "Could not set the expiration time for the fill reject for order:" + toString(), e);
4796                //continue as this is not critical.
4797            }
4798        }
4799 
4800        if (getRemainingQuantity() == 0)
4801        {
4802            setState(OrderStates.FILL);
4803        }
4804 
4805        if (Log.isDebugOn())
4806        {
4807            Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got filled with report with exchange/execId (" + exchangeExecIdString + ") for " + totalQuantity + " contracts");
4808        }
4809 
4810        return report;
4811    }
4812 
4813    /**
4814     * This is used to cancel the order when Satisfaction order disposition is given by NBBO Agent. Cancel reason will not be provided here.
4815     *
4816     * @param disposition
4817     */
4818    public int cancelWithDisposition(short disposition)
4819    {
4820        return orderCancel.cancelWithDisposition(this, disposition);
4821    }
4822 
4823    public ExtensionsHelper getExtensionsHelper(String someExtensions, String errLogReason)
4824    {
4825        ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = null;
4826 
4827        try
4828        {
4829            extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(someExtensions);
4830        }
4831        catch (Exception e)
4832        {
4833            Log.exception(this, "Unable to parse incoming "+errLogReason+" string: " + someExtensions +
4834                    " for order (" + getOrderIdString() + ") - creating default extensions helper", e);
4835        }
4836        finally
4837        {
4838            if (extensionsHelper == null)
4839            {
4840                extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper();
4841            }
4842        }
4843 
4844        return extensionsHelper;
4845    }

4848    {
4849        try
4850        {
4851            helper.setValue(key, value);
4852        }
4853        catch (java.text.ParseException e)
4854        {
4855            Log.exception("Order: Parse exception while trying to set value in extensions helper.  Value not set.", e);
4856        }
4857    }

4883    private String getExchangeExecIdString(String reportExtensions)
4884    {
4885        String execId = EMPTY_STRING;
4886        String exchangeString;
4887 
4888        // Create an extensions helper for the fill report.
4889        ExtensionsHelper fillExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(reportExtensions, "for report");
4890 
4891        switch (getSource())
4892        {
4893            case Sources.LINKAGE:
4894            case Sources.ITS:
4895            case InternalOrderSources.STOCKFIXLINKAGE:
4896                // Get the exec ID
4897                execId = fillExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.CBOE_EXEC_ID);
4898 
4899                // Set the exchange string (for logging the exec id)
4900                exchangeString = ExchangeStrings.CBOE;
4901 
4902                break;
4903 
4904            default: // must be a CBOE source, exec ID is from elsewhere
4905 
4906                // Get the away exchange exec Id.
4907                execId = fillExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.AWAY_EXCHANGE_EXEC_ID);
4908 
4909                // Get the away exchange; set it (for logging the exec id)
4910                ExtensionsHelper orderExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(getExtensions(), "for order");
4911                exchangeString = orderExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXCHANGE_DESTINATION);
4912        }
4913 
4914        return exchangeString + "/" + execId.toString();
4915    }
4916 
4917    public String getExecutingExchange()
4918    {
4919        String executingExchange = null;
4920        switch (getSource())
4921        {
4922            case Sources.LINKAGE:
4923            case Sources.ITS:
4924            case InternalOrderSources.STOCKFIXLINKAGE:
4925                executingExchange = ExchangeStrings.CBOE;
4926                break;
4927            default:
4928                ExtensionsHelper orderExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(getExtensions(), "for order");
4929                executingExchange = orderExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXCHANGE_DESTINATION);
4930        }
4931        return executingExchange;
4932    }

4952    /**
4953     *  an order needs NBBO protection if
4954     *  1. it is a customer order
4955     *  2. it request for NBBO protection
4956     *  3. NBBO protection is not overriden. NBBO protection can be overriden if
4957     *      > when order is received, the order is not marketable agaist NBBO, in this case
4958     *        the NBBO protection request is automatically overriden
4959     *      > NBBO agent decides to do so
4960     */
4961    public boolean needsNBBOProtection()
4962    {
4963 
4964        return isOrderConfiguredToHaveNBBOProtection() && ! isNBBOProtectionOverriden();
4965    }
4966 
4967    private boolean isOrderConfiguredToHaveNBBOProtection()
4968    {
4969            if (isLightOrder())
4970            {
4971                    return isNBBOProtectionRequested();
4972            }
4973        try
4974        {
4975            boolean linkageEnable = getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getTradingPropertyLinkageEnabledFlag();
4976            if (! linkageEnable)
4977            {
4978                return false;
4979            }
4980        }
4981        catch (NotFoundException e)
4982        {
4983            Log.alarm(this, " Could not find the linkage enabled flag for order:" + getOrderIdString());
4984            return false;
4985        }
4986 
4987        short contingencyType = getContingencyType();
4988        
4989        if( contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP ||
4990                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP_BOOK ||
4991                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.CASH_CROSS ||
4992                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.NEXT_DAY_CROSS ||
4993                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.TWO_DAY_CROSS  ||
4994                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.TIED_CROSS_SWEEP)
4995        {
4996            return false;
4997        }
4998 
4999        // Internal synthetic order for cross product leg will not need NBBO protection processing
5000        if(getOrderOriginType() == InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER)
5001        {
5002            return false;
5003        }
5004        
5005        String strategy = getMyHome().getIppProcessingStrategy(getActiveSession());
5006 
5007        if (strategy == null)
5008        {
5009            return false;
5010        }
5011 
5012        if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_NONE))
5013        {
5014            return false;
5015        }
5016        else if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_IPP_REQUIRED)  && allowTradeAndShip())
5017        {
5018            return true;
5019        }
5020        else
5021        if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_IF_CUSTOMER_REQUIRES)  && allowTradeAndShip() && isNBBOProtectionRequested())
5022        {
5023            return true;
5024        }
5025 
5026        return false;
5027    }

5054    /**
5055     * Note: if the new state is ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT, the order is marked with hadNBBOProtection
5056     * true
5057     */
5058    public short changeToState(short aNewState)
5059    {
5060        short oldState = getState();
5061 
5062        if (Log.isDebugOn())
5063        {
5064            Log.debug(this, "changing order state - from: " + oldState + " to: " + aNewState);
5065        }
5066 
5067        if (aNewState == InternalOrderStates.ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT)
5068        {
5069            setHadNBBOProtection(true);
5070        }
5071        else if (aNewState == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY) {
5072            setHandlingInstruction(null);
5073        }
5074        setState(aNewState);
5075 
5076        return oldState;
5077    }

5375    public void fillPendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, char billingType) throws DataValidationException
5376    {
5377        validatePendingTrade(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, false); //false indicates this is just a sub pending trade
5378        int pendingTradeQuantity = getPendingTradeQuantity();
5379        if (pendingTradeQuantity == 0)
5380        {
5381            setPendingTradeQuantity(pendingTradeQuantity + quantity);
5382            setPendingTradePrice(aPrice);
5383            setPendingTradeId(tradeId);
5384        }
5385        else
5386        {
5387            setPendingTradeQuantity(pendingTradeQuantity + quantity);
5388        }
5389    }

5392     * complete a pending trade
5393     */
5394    public FilledReportStruct completePendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, char billingType)
5395    throws DataValidationException
5396    {
5397        validatePendingTrade(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, true); //true indicates this is a completion call
5398        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
5399        setPendingTradePrice(null);
5400        setPendingTradeId(0);
5401        FilledReportStruct report = doOrderFill(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, contraParties, billingType);
5402        return report;
5403    }

5405    /**
5406     * validate pending trade
5407     */
5408    private void validatePendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, boolean inCompletion)
5409    throws DataValidationException
5410    {
5411        String logMSG;
5412        if (getPrimitiveProductKey() != product)
5413        {
5414            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> pending fill product key does not match order productkey" + product + ":" + getPrimitiveProductKey();
5415            Log.alarm(logMSG);
5416            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
5417        }
5418        if (getPendingTradeQuantity() == 0)
5419        {
5420            return; //order is not in a pending trade yet
5421        }
5422        if (tradeId != getPendingTradeId())
5423        {
5424            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Order can only participate in one pending at any given time " + toString();
5425            Log.alarm(logMSG);
5426            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TRADE_TYPE);
5427        }
5428        if (aPrice != getPendingTradePrice())
5429        {
5430            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Sub-pending trades can only occur at the same price in one pending trade " + toString();
5431            Log.alarm(logMSG);
5432            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRICE);
5433        }
5434        if (inCompletion && quantity != getPendingTradeQuantity())
5435        {
5436            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Pending trade quantity has to be the same as the sum of quantities of all sub-pending trades";
5437            Log.alarm(logMSG);
5438            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
5439        }
5440 
5441    }
5442 
5443    /**
5444     * To return the OrderBookStruct from the Order.
5445     *
5446     * @return com.cboe.idl.cmiIntermarketMessages.OrderBookStruct
5447     * author Sandip Chatterjee
5448     */

5450    {

5452

5517    private String getSessionClearingAcronymInProfile(SessionProfileUserDefinitionStruct userStruct)
5518    {
5519        String acr = UNDEFINED;
5520 
5521        if (allowUseClearingAcronymConfigured() && (userStruct != null) && (userStruct.role != UserRoles.MARKET_MAKER))
5522        {
5523            // sessionClearingAcronym is used by Non MarketMaker's order only
5524            // if it is with Market maker role, do nothing
5525            if (Log.isDebugOn())
5526            {
5527                Log.debug(this, "trying to find the default clearing acronym for user: " + userStruct.userId  + ", sessionName: " + getActiveSession() + " for order: " + toString());
5528            }
5529            for (int i = 0; i < userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms.length; i++)
5530            {
5531                if (getActiveSession().equals(userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionName))
5532                {
5533                   acr = userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym;
5534                   if (Log.isDebugOn())
5535                   {
5536                       Log.debug(this, "Needs to overwrite the clearingAcr to: " + userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym +
5537                                       ", of user: " + userStruct.userId + ", sessionName: " + getActiveSession() + " for order: " + toString());
5538                   }
5539                   break;
5540                }
5541                if (SessionNameValues.ALL_SESSION_NAME.equals(userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionName))
5542                {
5543                    acr = userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym;
5544                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
5545                    {
5546                        Log.debug(this, "Needs to overwrite the clearingAcr to: " + userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym +
5547                                        ", of user: " + userStruct.userId + ", sessionName: " + SessionNameValues.ALL_SESSION_NAME + " for order: " + toString());
5548                    }
5549                }
5550            }
5551        }
5552        return acr;
5553    }

5568    /**
5569     * Calculates the acronym name for  clearing purpose from profile.clearingAcronym.
5570     * Originator will be used if is for ICM order.  For Other order, if not MM, will try
5571     * to use Broker's clearingAcronym.
5572     *
5573     * @return  The originator acronym if is ICM
5574     *          The Broker's clearingAcronym
5575     *          default if broker has not configured to use the feature.
5576     */
5577    public ExchangeAcronymStruct getClearingAcronym(short tradeContext, boolean isTradeWithManualQuote)
5578    {
5579        ExchangeAcronymStruct tmpUserAcronym = getUserAcronym(); // default to use first
5580 
5581        //If it is an auction trade then ONLY for internalized or matched order return different executing broker
5582        if (tradeContext == TradeContext.AUCTION_TRADE && (isInternalizedOrder() || isFirmMatchOrder()))
5583        {
5584            return getInternalizationAuctionTradeBroker();
5585        }
5586 
5587        String acr = tmpUserAcronym.acronym;
5588        SessionProfileUserDefinitionStruct userStruct = null;
5589        try
5590        {
5591            // if clears like quote use originator's setup (new requirement for I-order 2-25-04), otherwise use user's setup
5592            // WR #6208: manul quote's clearning acronym is its originator's acronym
5593            if (clearsLikeQuote() || isManualQuote())
5594            {
5595                tmpUserAcronym = getOriginatorAcronym(); // this could be the use or the originator is has one
5596                acr =  tmpUserAcronym.acronym;
5597                if (Log.isDebugOn())
5598                {
5599                   Log.debug(this, "Found I-order Originator User(" + tmpUserAcronym.exchange + "-" + tmpUserAcronym.acronym + ") for the operator userId(" + getUserId() + ") for order: " + toString());
5600                }
5601            }
5602            else
5603            {
5604                userStruct = getUserMaintenanceService().getSessionProfileUserByUserId(getUserId());
5605                String newAcr =  getSessionClearingAcronymInProfile(userStruct);
5606                if (UNDEFINED.equals(newAcr) && getMyHome().isAnonymousTradingIfNotClearsLikeQuote())
5607                {
5608                    newAcr = getMyHome().getAnonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker();
5609                }
5610 
5611                if (UNDEFINED.equals(newAcr)  || NOT_APPLICABLE.equals(newAcr))
5612                {
5613                    // Session specific default clearing Acr is not defined for User
5614                    // and anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker is not ON or configured in XML either
5615                    // use the submitter user acr of the order, e.g. don't over-ride it with anything.
5616                    newAcr = acr;
5617                }
5618                else if (isTradeWithManualQuote)
5619                {
5620                    // if order trade with manual quote, 
5621                    newAcr = getMyHome().getManualQuoteContraOrderBroker();   
5622                }
5623                tmpUserAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(getUserAcronym().exchange, newAcr);
5624            }
5625        }
5626        catch (Exception e)
5627        {
5628            Log.exception(this, "Cannot get user in getClearingAcronym() from userMaintenanceService by UserId(" + acr + ")", e);
5629        }
5630 
5631        return tmpUserAcronym;
5632     }

5779    public boolean isSalable()
5780    {
5781        try {
5782            TradingClass theClass = this.getTradingProduct().getTradingClass();
5783            if (theClass.getIndexHybridIndicator() && 
5784                    FirmTradingPropertyHelper.isNewBOBLinkage(activeSession, this.classKey, this.productKey) ) {
5785                AllowedSalOriginCodes[] salOriginCodes = theClass.getAllowedSALOriginCodesList();
5786                if (null != salOriginCodes) {
5787                    for (AllowedSalOriginCodes theOriginCode : salOriginCodes) {
5788                        if (orderOriginType == theOriginCode.getDisplayAllowedSalOriginCode() ) {
5789                            return theOriginCode.getDisplayAllowedSalOriginCodeEnabledFlag();
5790                        }
5791                    }
5792                }
5793                return false;
5794            }
5795            else {
5796        String[] salableCodes = getMyHome().getSalableCodes();
5797        if (null != salableCodes)
5798        {
5799            for (int i = 0; i < salableCodes.length; i++)
5800            {
5801                if (getOrderOriginType() == salableCodes[i].charAt(0))
5802                {
5803                    return true;
5804                }
5805            }
5806        }
5807       /*
5808        * Additionally we will check for C or W type origin codes
5809        * for bob classes
5810        */
5811        return isCustomerTypeForBobClasses();
5812    }
5813        }
5814        catch (Exception exe) {

5891     * or opposite auction price

5895     * 1) the Order is IOC Quote-like and remaining qty is cancelled or

5903 
5904    /**
5905     *
5906     * @param self
5907     * @param needsToCheckMKT
5908     * @param book
5909     * @return
5910     * @throws DataValidationException
5911     */
5912    private boolean cancelIOCQuoteLikeOrder(Order self, boolean needsToCheckMKT, OrderBook book) throws DataValidationException
5913    {
5914        int qtyToCancel = getRemainingQuantity();
5915        if ( qtyToCancel <= 0)
5916        {
5917            return true;
5918        }
5919        boolean bookIt = false;
5920        if (getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.IOC)
5921        {
5922                if (book != null && needsToCheckMKT)
5923                {
5924                    bookIt = shouldRemainBooked(book);
5925                }
5926                if (!bookIt)
5927                {
5928                    if (isBooked())
5929                    {
5930                        unbookOrder(self, book, qtyToCancel);
5931                    }
5932                    // have to cancel the IOC order,
5933                    // because the current MKT condition doesn't allow to book it
5934                    cancel(ActivityReasons.USER);
5935                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
5936                    {
5937                        Log.debug("Cancelled and unbooked IOC I order's remaning qty : " + qtyToCancel
5938                                + ", OrderId = " + OrderImpl.orderIdToString(getOrderId()));
5939                    }
5940                    return true;
5941                }
5942        }
5943        return false;
5944    }
5945

5947    {
5948        return TradeHelper.isMarketable(this, book);
5949    }

6118    public int getDisplayQuantity()
6119    {
6120                   setDisplayQuantity();

6122    }
6123 
6124    private void setDisplayQuantity()
6125    {
6126        if( getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE )
6127        {
6128            //Any variable prefixed with "prev" means it holds the value
6129            //that existed prior to changing the order's quantity.
6130            //for example, prevDisplayQuantity is the quantity that was 
6131            //displayed before a trade, now we are updating the display
6132            //quantity to reflect the trade.
6133            final int newRemainingQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
6134            final int displayContingency = getContingencyVolume();
6135            int lotSize = getLotSize();
6136            int delta = newRemainingQuantity - prevRemainingQuantity;
6137            if (isDeltaOddAndOrderFlashing(delta, newRemainingQuantity, lotSize))
6138            {
6139                return;
6140            }
6141            if (displayQuantity>0 && isBooked())
6142            {
6143                if ((newRemainingQuantity==prevRemainingQuantity) && (displayQuantity <= newRemainingQuantity))
6144                {
6145                    return;
6146                }
6147 
6148                displayQuantity += delta;                
6149                         
6150                int replenishThreshhold = getReserveOrderRefreshSize()* lotSize;
6151                
6152                if ((displayQuantity <= displayContingency) && (displayQuantity > replenishThreshhold) && (displayQuantity <= newRemainingQuantity))
6153                {
6154                        adjustOddLotDisplay( lotSize );
6155                    return;
6156                }
6157            }
6158            
6159            displayQuantity = Math.min( newRemainingQuantity, displayContingency);
6160            
6161            adjustOddLotDisplay( lotSize );
6162            
6163            int newReservedQuantity = newRemainingQuantity - displayQuantity;
6164            if( newRemainingQuantity>0 && newReservedQuantity < prevReservedQuantity )  //reserved quauntity is now displayed
6165            {
6166                hasReserveQuantityDisplayed = true;
6167            }               
6168        }
6169        else
6170        {
6171            displayQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
6172            if (treatedLikeQuote())
6173                displayQuantity = LotCalculator.roundLotPortion(displayQuantity, getLotSize());
6174                
6175        }
6176    }
6177    
6178    private final boolean isDeltaOddAndOrderFlashing(int delta, int newRemQty, int lotSize)
6179    {
6180        //delta is an oddPortion
6181        // It is flashing
6182        // There is still a remaining round portion
6183        if((isIPPExposing() || getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_EXPOSING)  
6184           && LotCalculator.isOddLot(Math.abs(delta), lotSize)
6185           && newRemQty >= lotSize)
6186        {
6187            //If tradable is a reserve odd lot flash termination
6188            //do nothing
6189            return true;
6190        }
6191        return false;
6192    }
6193    
6194    private final void adjustOddLotDisplay( int lotSize )
6195    {
6196       // If displayQuantity > lotSize and has odd portion remove that oddPortion
6197       if (displayQuantity > lotSize)
6198       {
6199           //OddPortion is only displayed if there is no remaining round quantity    
6200           int roundLot = lotSize == 1 ? displayQuantity : LotCalculator.roundLotPortion(displayQuantity, lotSize);
6201           int oddLot = displayQuantity - roundLot;
6202           if (oddLot > 0)
6203           {
6204              displayQuantity -= oddLot;
6205           }
6206       }
6207    }

6211        return prevReservedQuantity;
6212    }

6214    public int getPrevDisplayedQuantity()
6215    {
6216            return prevDisplayedQuantity;
6217    }
6218    
6219    /**
6220     * WARMING:
6221     * This method is implemented in a way that there could be one and only one caller,
6222     *      which currently is the OrderBookPriceItem,
6223     *          as it totally rely on the accurate sequence of pre-cur-pre-cur-...
6224     *             to guarantee correct book depth summary
6225     *      This method is called every time AFTER the prev* are used,
6226     *          and the cur* become the prev* for later
6227     */
6228    public void savePreviousReserve()
6229    {       
6230            if(getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE)
6231        {
6232                    //Any variable prefixed with "prev" means it holds the value
6233                    //that existed prior to changing the order's quantity.
6234                    //for example, prevDisplayQuantity is the quantity that was 
6235                    //displayed before a trade, now we are updating the display
6236                    //quantity to reflect the trade.
6237                    prevRemainingQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
6238                    prevDisplayedQuantity = displayQuantity;
6239                    prevReservedQuantity = prevRemainingQuantity - prevDisplayedQuantity;
6240        }
6241    }

6285    public void fill(FilledReportStruct[] filledReports, int startIndex)
6286    throws DataValidationException{
6287        LegOrderDetail legDetail = null;
6288        int preProductKey = -1;
6289        
6290        if(startIndex >= filledReports.length)
6291        {
6292            setTransactionSequenceNumber(filledReports[filledReports.length -1].transactionSequenceNumber);
6293        }
6294        
6295        for (int i=startIndex;i<filledReports.length;i++)
6296        {
6297            FilledReportStruct fill=filledReports[i];
6298            try
6299            {
6300                //for potential use of multiple leg fills
6301                if (fill.productKey != preProductKey)
6302                {
6303                   legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(fill.productKey);
6304                   preProductKey = fill.productKey;
6305                }
6306                fill.transactionSequenceNumber = incrementSequenceNumber();
6307                fill.fillReportType = ReportTypes.STRATEGY_LEG_REPORT;
6308                legDetail.setFill(fill);
6309            }
6310            catch (Exception e)
6311            {
6312                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
6313                        "not found the leg with product key = " + productKey + " of strategy "
6314                                + getPrimitiveProductKey() + ": " + e.getMessage(), 0);
6315            }
6316        }
6317    }

6329    public void publishAuctionEvent(AuctionHistoryStruct p_auctionInfo)
6330    {
6331        OrderHomeImpl orderHome = getMyHome(); 
6332        com.cboe.idl.order.OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs = buildOrderHistoryDetailStructs();
6333        
6334        // for new HAL, we need to reflect the last trade into the NBBO. Not changing IDL for timing issue
6335        // so override NBBOStruct based on book
6336        if (p_auctionInfo.auctionType == InternalAuctionTypes.AUCTION_NEW_HAL  && 
6337                        p_auctionInfo.auctionEventType == ActivityTypes.AUCTION_START) {
6338                overrideNBBOForHAL(ordHistoryStructs[0].quoteQueryForPackageAndLegs.quoteQueryV2Struct, p_auctionInfo.productKey);
6339        }
6340        orderHome.getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptAuctionEvent.getEventType() ).acceptAuctionEvent(
6341                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(), getOrderId(),
6342                p_auctionInfo, getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
6343                ordHistoryStructs);
6344      
6345        if (Log.isDebugOn())
6346        {
6347            Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderId() + " got auction for " + p_auctionInfo.quantityTradedInAuction + " contracts");
6348        }        
6349    }
6350    
6351    
6352    /**
6353     * Override NBBOStruct if CBOE is no longer NBBO
6354     * This could happen because a trade is already exceuted 
6355     * but current market hasn't been updated yet
6356     * 
6357     * OrderImpl
6358     * @param quoteQueryV2Struct
6359     * @param productKey
6360     * void
6361     */
6362    private void overrideNBBOForHAL(com.cboe.idl.marketData.QuoteQueryV2Struct quoteQueryV2Struct, int productKey)
6363    {
6364            OrderBook orderBook;
6365            try {
6366                    orderBook = getMyHome().getOrderBook(productKey);
6367            } catch(DataValidationException dve) {
6368                    Log.alarm("Failed to overrideNBBOForHAL. Can't get OrderBook for product: " + productKey);
6369                    return;
6370            }
6371            
6372            BestBookStruct bestBookStruct = orderBook.getBestBook().toNonContingentStruct();
6373            Price bboAskPrice = PriceFactory.create(bestBookStruct.askPrice);
6374            Price bboBidPrice = PriceFactory.create(bestBookStruct.bidPrice);
6375            NBBOStruct nbboStruct = quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct;
6376            NBBOStruct botrStruct = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct;
6377            Price botrAskPrice = PriceFactory.create(botrStruct.askPrice);
6378            Price botrBidPrice = PriceFactory.create(botrStruct.bidPrice);
6379            String CBOEExchangeName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getSession(bestBookStruct.sessionName).exchangeAcronym;
6380            // if CBOE is no longer NBBO, take BOTR for NBBO
6381            if (nbboStruct.bidExchangeVolume.length == 1 && 
6382                            nbboStruct.bidExchangeVolume[0].exchange.equals(CBOEExchangeName) &&
6383                            new BuySide().isFirstBetter(botrBidPrice, bboBidPrice)) {
6384                    // populate BOTR to NBBO
6385                    quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidPrice = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidPrice;
6386                    quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidExchangeVolume = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidExchangeVolume;
6387            }
6388            
6389            if (nbboStruct.askExchangeVolume.length == 1 && 
6390                            nbboStruct.askExchangeVolume[0].exchange.equals(CBOEExchangeName) &&
6391                            new SellSide().isFirstBetter(botrAskPrice, bboAskPrice)) {
6392                    // populate BOTR to NBBO
6393                    quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.askPrice = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.askPrice;
6394                    quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.askExchangeVolume = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.askExchangeVolume;
6395            }
6396    }
6397    
6398    public OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] buildOrderHistoryDetailStructsForFR() {
6399        epBuildOrderHistoryStructs.enter();
6400        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] orderHistoryDetailStructArray = null;
6401        OrderHistoryDetailStruct[] orderHistoryDetailStruct = null;
6402        int[] productKeysOnLegsNPackage = new int[legOrderDetails.length+1];
6403        productKeysOnLegsNPackage[0] = getPrimitiveProductKey();
6404        try
6405        {
6406            if (getProductType() == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
6407            {  
6408                for (int i=0; i< legOrderDetails.length; i++)
6409                {  
6410                    productKeysOnLegsNPackage[i+1] = legOrderDetails[i].getProductKey();
6411                }
6412            }
6413        orderHistoryDetailStructArray = getMyHome().buildOrderHistoryDetailStructsForFR(getActiveSession(), productKeysOnLegsNPackage);
6414        return orderHistoryDetailStructArray ;
6415        }
6416        finally
6417        {
6418            epBuildOrderHistoryStructs.exit(false);
6419        }
6420 
6421    }

6459    public boolean isDeltaNeutral() throws NotFoundException, SystemException
6460    {
6461        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
6462        boolean stockFlag = false;
6463        int legPriceCount = 0;
6464        // Atleast one leg should be an Equity
6465        for(int i =0; i< legs.length; i++)
6466        {
6467            ProductData legProdData = getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(legs[i].getProductKey());
6468            if(legProdData.getProductType() == ProductTypes.EQUITY || legProdData.getProductType() == ProductTypes.INDEX) 
6469            {
6470                stockFlag = true;
6471            }                       
6472            legPriceCount = legs[i].getMustUsePrice().isValuedPrice()?(legPriceCount+1):legPriceCount;
6473                         
6474        }
6475        
6476        boolean noOrderPrice = getPrice().isNoPrice()? true: false;
6477        
6478        return stockFlag && noOrderPrice && (legPriceCount == legs.length);
6479    }

6501    public String[] getUserIdsFromUserkeys() 
6502    {
6503       String[] dAIMUserIds = new String[this.dAIMedUserList.size()];
6504       for(int i =0; i<dAIMedUserList.size(); i++)
6505       {
6506           try
6507           {
6508               dAIMUserIds[i] = findUserId(dAIMedUserList.get(i).intValue());
6509           }
6510           catch (SystemException e)
6511           {
6512               // don't do anything, no user info available... publish empty string
6513               dAIMUserIds[i] = "";
6514           }
6515            catch (DataValidationException e)
6516            {
6517                // don't do anything, no user info available... publish empty string
6518                dAIMUserIds[i] = "";
6519            }
6520       }
6521       return dAIMUserIds;
6522    }

6613    public boolean needCancelReForUpdate(OrderHandlingStruct update)
6614    {
6615        Price newPrice = PriceFactory.create(update.price);
6616        if (!newPrice.equals(getPrice())) return true;
6617        
6618        if (update.orderOriginType != getOrderOriginType()) return true;
6619        
6620        if (update.side != getSide().toSideValue()) return true;
6621        
6622        if (update.contingency.type != getContingencyType()) return true;
6623 
6624        int newQuantity = update.originalQuantity;
6625        if (newQuantity > getQuantityAllowed()) return true;
6626 
6627        return false;
6628    }

6747    public boolean isProtected()
6748    {

6754                (origin == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT
6755                || origin == OrderOrigins.BROKER_DEALER
6756                || origin == OrderOrigins.CUSTOMER
6757                || origin == OrderOrigins.FIRM_FBW_ICM
6758                || origin == OrderOrigins.BROKER_DEALER_FBW_NON_CUSTOMER)&&
6759                !this.isOddLot());
6760    }

7135    private void setOrderSide(char order_side) 
7136    {
7137        if(this.order_side == null)
7138        {
7139            switch(order_side)
7140            {
7141                case Sides.BUY : 
7142                    this.order_side = BUY_SIDE;
7143                    break;
7144                case Sides.SELL :
7145                case Sides.SELL_SHORT :
7146                case Sides.SELL_SHORT_EXEMPT :
7147                    this.order_side = SELL_SIDE;
7148                    break;
7149                case Sides.AS_DEFINED : 
7150                    this.order_side = AS_DEFINED_SIDE;
7151                    break;
7152                case Sides.OPPOSITE :
7153                    this.order_side = OPPOSITE_SIDE;
7154                    break;
7155            }
7156        }
7157    }

7165 
7166    private OrderImplTXChangeLog getCurrentTXLog()
7167    {
7168        TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionLog = Transaction.getCallbackSession().getCurrentTransaction();
7169        TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionParentLog = Transaction.getCallbackSession().getCurrentTransaction().getParentTransaction();
7170        markOrderFieldChanged();
7171        OrderImplTXChangeLog tmpOrderImplTXChangeLog = (OrderImplTXChangeLog) getCurrentTXLog(owRequestedTransactionLog, firstOrderImplTXChangeLog, orderImplTXChangeLog);
7172 
7173        if(tmpOrderImplTXChangeLog == null)
7174        {
7175 
7176            linkMissingOWTransactionLog(owRequestedTransactionLog, owRequestedTransactionParentLog);
7177 
7178            OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
7179            currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(owRequestedTransactionLog);
7180            if(owRequestedTransactionLog != null)
7181            {
7182                currentOrderTXLog.setOwParentTxLog(owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction());
7183            }
7184            currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(orderImplTXChangeLog);
7185            if(orderImplTXChangeLog != null)
7186            {
7187                orderImplTXChangeLog.setChildTXChangeLog(currentOrderTXLog);
7188            }
7189 
7190            orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
7191        }
7192 
7193        if(firstOrderImplTXChangeLog == null)
7194        {
7195            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = orderImplTXChangeLog;
7196        }
7197 
7198        //Log.information("ORDERID: " + this.getOrderIdString() + "OrdeRImpl.getCurrentTXLog >>> FirstTX Log: " + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog + ":" + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog() + ":" + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog.getOwParentTxLog());
7199        //Log.information("ORDERID: " + this.getOrderIdString() + "OrdeRImpl.getCurrentTXLog >>> Current OrderTX Log Log: " + orderImplTXChangeLog + ":" + orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog() + ":" + orderImplTXChangeLog.getOwParentTxLog());
7200        return orderImplTXChangeLog;
7201    }
7202 
7203    private void linkMissingOWTransactionLog(TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionLog,
7204            TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionParentLog)
7205    {
7206        if(orderImplTXChangeLog == null && owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction() != null)
7207        {
7208            TransactionLog tempOWTXLog = owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction();
7209            while(tempOWTXLog != null)
7210            {
7211                if(tempOWTXLog.getParentTransaction() == null)
7212                {
7213                    break;
7214                }
7215                tempOWTXLog = tempOWTXLog.getParentTransaction();
7216            } //end while loop
7217            
7218            TransactionLog currentCachedOWTXLog = tempOWTXLog;
7219 
7220            //Create OrderImplTXLog for Root Transaction
7221            OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
7222            currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(tempOWTXLog);
7223            currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(null);
7224            orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
7225            
7226            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = orderImplTXChangeLog;       //set the First TX log.     
7227        }
7228        
7229        if(orderImplTXChangeLog != null)
7230        {
7231            TransactionLog currentCachedOWTXLog = orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog();
7232            while(currentCachedOWTXLog != null && currentCachedOWTXLog != owRequestedTransactionParentLog)
7233            {
7234                if(currentCachedOWTXLog.getSubTransaction() == owRequestedTransactionLog)
7235                {
7236                    break;
7237                }
7238                OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
7239                currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(currentCachedOWTXLog.getSubTransaction());
7240                currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(orderImplTXChangeLog);
7241                orderImplTXChangeLog.setChildTXChangeLog(currentOrderTXLog);
7242                orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
7243                currentCachedOWTXLog = orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog();
7244            }
7245        }
7246    }
7247

7251    {
7252        super.commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
7253        firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = null;
7254        orderImplTXChangeLog = null;
7255        changesCommitted();
7256    }

7258    private void rollbackOrderFieldChanges()
7259    {
7260        boolean isRootTransactionRollback = super.rollbackFieldChanges(this, firstOrderImplTXChangeLog, orderImplTXChangeLog);
7261 
7262        if(isRootTransactionRollback)
7263        {
7264            super.commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
7265            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = null;
7266            orderImplTXChangeLog = null;
7267        }
7268    }
7269 
7270 
7271    /**
7272     * This method registers for the Transaction Listener if the object
7273     * is not marked dirty and does not contains any changes. If it is
7274     * already marked dirty then this method do nothing. The pusrpose is
7275     * to register the transaction Listener only once for this object during
7276     * the current transaction. The object is marked clean (not dirty) on
7277     * commit(after saving changes) or rollback (after undoing the changes).
7278     */
7279    public void markOrderFieldChanged()
7280    {
7281        if(!isObjectMarkedDirty())  //Already marked dirty object and register for the Transaction Lisenter
7282        {
7283            setObjectMarkedDirty(true);
7284            Transaction.registerListener(new TransactionListener()
7285             {
7286                public void commitEvent()
7287                {
7288                    commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
7289                }
7290                public void rollbackEvent()
7291                {
7292                }
7293             }
7294            );
7295 
7296            Transaction.registerRollbackListenerWithPriority( BOSessionManager.getDefaultManager().getSession(), new TransactionListener()
7297            {
7298                public void commitEvent()
7299                {
7300                }
7301 
7302                public void rollbackEvent()
7303                {
7304                    rollbackOrderFieldChanges();
7305                }
7306            }
7307            );
7308        }
7309    }

7361            {
7362                    byte[] newReqBuffer = LightOrderBuffer.getThreadLocalInstance().getLastDecodedBuffer();
7363                    if (newReqBuffer != null)
7364                    {

7366                            {
7367                                    Log.debug("LO NEW: " + getBranch() + ":" + getBranchSequenceNumber() + ":" + getOrderId().highCboeId + ":" + getOrderId().lowCboeId + ":" + orderKey);
7368                            }
7369                                incrementSequenceNumber(); // should be 1 now.
7370//                                long highLowId = orderId.highCboeId << 16 |orderId.lowCboeId;
7371                                getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptLightOrder.getEventType()).acceptLightOrder(
7372                                                getRoutingStruct().groups[0], orderKey, sourceReceivedTime, newReqBuffer, orderId.correspondentFirm);                                                            
7373                    }
7374            }
